access logger implementations and configuration definitions in Envoy v1.31.2. The analysis categorizes each logger by whether it supports structured (JSON) logging or only unstructured text logging.\\n\\n### Access Logger Implementations and JSON/Structured Logging Support\\n\\n#### 1. File Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.file)\\n**Support: YES - Full structured logging support**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/file/config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`\\n- Supported formats:\\n  - Plain text format (deprecated `format` field)\\n  - JSON format via `json_format` (google.protobuf.Struct, all values as strings)\\n  - Typed JSON format via `typed_json_format` (values as strings, numbers, booleans)\\n  - Modern format via `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString supporting JSON)\\n- Allows configuration of JSON structures with field substitution using Envoy's command operators\\n\\n#### 2. Fluentd Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.fluentd)\\n**Support: YES - Structured JSON-based logging**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc`, `fluentd_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`\\n- Format: Uses JSON formatting (via `createJsonFormatter`) which is then serialized to MessagePack for Fluentd Forward Protocol\\n- Record structure: Defined as `google.protobuf.Struct` with field values derived from access log command operators\\n- Supports nested JSON objects from command operators like FILTER_STATE and DYNAMIC_METADATA\\n\\n#### 3. gRPC Access Log Service (envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc / envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc)\\n**Support: YES - Structured protobuf logging**\\n- HTTP Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_config.cc`, `http_grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- TCP Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_config.cc`, `tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n- Format: Uses StreamAccessLogsMessage protobuf structure containing:\\n  - For HTTP: HTTPRequestProperties, HTTPResponseProperties, and HTTPAccessLogEntry\\n  - For TCP: TCPAccessLogEntry\\n- Inherently structured via protobuf messages (not text-based)\\n- Supports custom tags and filter state object serialization\\n\\n#### 4. OpenTelemetry Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry)\\n**Support: YES - Structured OpenTelemetry protocol logging**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/config.cc`, `access_log_impl.cc`, `http_access_log_impl.cc`, `grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`\\n- Format: Uses OpenTelemetry Logs Protocol with structured fields:\\n  - `body`: AnyValue field for log message\\n  - `attributes`: KeyValueList for structured key-value pairs\\n  - `resource_attributes`: KeyValueList for resource metadata\\n- Supports both gRPC and HTTP/JSON transports for OTLP export\\n- Values are rendered as strings, numbers, or complex JSON objects via command operators\\n\\n#### 5. Stream Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.stdout / envoy.access_loggers.stderr)\\n**Support: YES - Flexible format support via SubstitutionFormatString**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`\\n- Format: Uses `config.core.v3.SubstitutionFormatString` which supports:\\n  - Text format (plain text with substitutions)\\n  - JSON format (via SubstitutionFormatString json_format)\\n- Default format: Envoy's standard text format\\n- Outputs to OS standard output or error streams\\n\\n#### 6. Stats Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.stats)\\n**Support: NO - Not a text or JSON logger**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/stats/config.cc`, `stats.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stats/v3/stats.proto`\\n- Format: Emits Envoy metrics/counters/histograms, not traditional access logs\\n- Metrics are tagged and values are derived from access log command operators\\n- Not comparable to JSON/structured text logging as it outputs metrics, not logs\\n\\n#### 7. WASM Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.wasm)\\n**Support: Implementation-defined**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/config.cc`, `wasm_access_log_impl.h`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`\\n- Format: Determined by the WASM plugin implementation\\n- Envoy passes request/response data and stream info to the WASM VM\\n- The WASM module decides how to format and output logs (could be JSON, text, or other formats)\\n\\n#### 8. Dynamic Modules Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.dynamic_modules)\\n**Support: Implementation-defined**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/config.cc`, `access_log.cc`, `access_log_config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto`\\n- Format: Determined by the dynamically-loaded module implementation\\n- Envoy loads shared objects (.so files) and passes access log context to the module's implementation\\n- The module can implement any logging format (JSON, text, binary, etc.)\\n- Configuration is passed as google.protobuf.Any and can include format hints (e.g., format: \\\"json\\\")\\n\\n### Access Log Filters (Supporting Infrastructure)\\nThese are filters that determine WHETHER to log, not HOW to format logs:\\n\\n#### 1. CEL Expression Filter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel)\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/cel.cc`, `config.cc`\\n- Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`\\n- Purpose: Evaluates CEL expressions to decide if access should be logged\\n\\n#### 2. Process Rate Limit Filter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.process_ratelimit)\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/filter.cc`, `config.cc`\\n- Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/v3/process_ratelimit.proto`\\n- Purpose: Rate-limits access log emission using global token buckets\\n\\n### Core/Common Infrastructure\\n\\n#### Access Log Framework (Core)\\n- `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.cc/h`: Core access log filter implementation and factory\\n- `source/common/access_log/access_log_manager_impl.cc/h`: Manages access log instances\\n- Provides: FilterFactory, StatusCodeFilter, DurationFilter, HeaderFilter, ResponseFlagFilter, GrpcStatusFilter, LogTypeFilter, MetadataFilter, and logical operators (AND, OR filters)\\n\\n#### Access Logger Common Base\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/access_log_base.cc/h`: Base class for access logger implementations\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/file_access_log_impl.cc/h`: Core file writing implementation\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger.h`: gRPC logger interface\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger_clients.h`: gRPC client management\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger_utils.cc/h`: gRPC utility functions\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/stream_access_log_common_impl.h`: Base for stream loggers\\n\\n### JSON/Structured Logging Support Summary\\n\\n**Full Structured Logging Support (Recommended):**\\n1. File Logger - Supports plain text, JSON, and typed JSON formats\\n2. Fluentd Logger - JSON with MessagePack serialization for nested objects\\n3. gRPC/ALS Logger - Protobuf-based structured messages\\n4. OpenTelemetry Logger - OTEL protocol with structured attributes and body\\n5. Stream Logger - Can output JSON via SubstitutionFormatString\\n\\n**Implementation-Defined:**\\n- WASM Logger - Format depends on plugin\\n- Dynamic Modules Logger - Format depends on loaded module\\n\\n**Not Applicable:**\\n- Stats Logger - Emits metrics, not logs\\n\\n**Infrastructure/Filtering Only:**\\n- CEL Filter - Controls which requests are logged\\n- Process Rate Limit Filter - Limits log emission rate\\n\\n### Key Observations\\n\\n1. **Modern Format Preference**: Envoy has shifted to `SubstitutionFormatString` (log_format field) as the modern standard for format configuration across File, Stream, and other loggers. This provides unified JSON/text format handling.\\n\\n2. **Structured Data Support**: All primary output loggers (File, Fluentd, gRPC/ALS, OpenTelemetry, Stream) support structured/JSON output. This provides comprehensive observability.\\n\\n3. **Nested Object Support**: Fluentd, gRPC/ALS, and OpenTelemetry support nested JSON objects via command operators like FILTER_STATE and DYNAMIC_METADATA.\\n\\n4. **Protocol-Based vs Text-Based**: gRPC/ALS and OpenTelemetry use binary protocols (gRPC + protobuf or OTLP) for structured data, while File, Fluentd, and Stream can use text-based JSON formats.\\n\\n5. **Extensibility**: WASM and Dynamic Modules provide plugin-based extensibility for custom logging implementations with any format.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2907,"cache_read_input_tokens":59500,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2907},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0cc18b1d-ea80-4e7d-8059-71758bd4b612","uuid":"53679d31-ea8b-413f-b5b5-78734fb1be97"}

access logger implementations and configuration definitions in Envoy v1.31.2. The analysis categorizes each logger by whether it supports structured (JSON) logging or only unstructured text logging.\\n\\n### Access Logger Implementations and JSON/Structured Logging Support\\n\\n#### 1. File Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.file)\\n**Support: YES - Full structured logging support**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/file/config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`\\n- Supported formats:\\n  - Plain text format (deprecated `format` field)\\n  - JSON format via `json_format` (google.protobuf.Struct, all values as strings)\\n  - Typed JSON format via `typed_json_format` (values as strings, numbers, booleans)\\n  - Modern format via `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString supporting JSON)\\n- Allows configuration of JSON structures with field substitution using Envoy's command operators\\n\\n#### 2. Fluentd Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.fluentd)\\n**Support: YES - Structured JSON-based logging**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc`, `fluentd_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`\\n- Format: Uses JSON formatting (via `createJsonFormatter`) which is then serialized to MessagePack for Fluentd Forward Protocol\\n- Record structure: Defined as `google.protobuf.Struct` with field values derived from access log command operators\\n- Supports nested JSON objects from command operators like FILTER_STATE and DYNAMIC_METADATA\\n\\n#### 3. gRPC Access Log Service (envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc / envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc)\\n**Support: YES - Structured protobuf logging**\\n- HTTP Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_config.cc`, `http_grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- TCP Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_config.cc`, `tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n- Format: Uses StreamAccessLogsMessage protobuf structure containing:\\n  - For HTTP: HTTPRequestProperties, HTTPResponseProperties, and HTTPAccessLogEntry\\n  - For TCP: TCPAccessLogEntry\\n- Inherently structured via protobuf messages (not text-based)\\n- Supports custom tags and filter state object serialization\\n\\n#### 4. OpenTelemetry Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry)\\n**Support: YES - Structured OpenTelemetry protocol logging**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/config.cc`, `access_log_impl.cc`, `http_access_log_impl.cc`, `grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`\\n- Format: Uses OpenTelemetry Logs Protocol with structured fields:\\n  - `body`: AnyValue field for log message\\n  - `attributes`: KeyValueList for structured key-value pairs\\n  - `resource_attributes`: KeyValueList for resource metadata\\n- Supports both gRPC and HTTP/JSON transports for OTLP export\\n- Values are rendered as strings, numbers, or complex JSON objects via command operators\\n\\n#### 5. Stream Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.stdout / envoy.access_loggers.stderr)\\n**Support: YES - Flexible format support via SubstitutionFormatString**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`\\n- Format: Uses `config.core.v3.SubstitutionFormatString` which supports:\\n  - Text format (plain text with substitutions)\\n  - JSON format (via SubstitutionFormatString json_format)\\n- Default format: Envoy's standard text format\\n- Outputs to OS standard output or error streams\\n\\n#### 6. Stats Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.stats)\\n**Support: NO - Not a text or JSON logger**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/stats/config.cc`, `stats.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stats/v3/stats.proto`\\n- Format: Emits Envoy metrics/counters/histograms, not traditional access logs\\n- Metrics are tagged and values are derived from access log command operators\\n- Not comparable to JSON/structured text logging as it outputs metrics, not logs\\n\\n#### 7. WASM Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.wasm)\\n**Support: Implementation-defined**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/config.cc`, `wasm_access_log_impl.h`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`\\n- Format: Determined by the WASM plugin implementation\\n- Envoy passes request/response data and stream info to the WASM VM\\n- The WASM module decides how to format and output logs (could be JSON, text, or other formats)\\n\\n#### 8. Dynamic Modules Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.dynamic_modules)\\n**Support: Implementation-defined**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/config.cc`, `access_log.cc`, `access_log_config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto`\\n- Format: Determined by the dynamically-loaded module implementation\\n- Envoy loads shared objects (.so files) and passes access log context to the module's implementation\\n- The module can implement any logging format (JSON, text, binary, etc.)\\n- Configuration is passed as google.protobuf.Any and can include format hints (e.g., format: \\\"json\\\")\\n\\n### Access Log Filters (Supporting Infrastructure)\\nThese are filters that determine WHETHER to log, not HOW to format logs:\\n\\n#### 1. CEL Expression Filter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel)\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/cel.cc`, `config.cc`\\n- Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`\\n- Purpose: Evaluates CEL expressions to decide if access should be logged\\n\\n#### 2. Process Rate Limit Filter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.process_ratelimit)\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/filter.cc`, `config.cc`\\n- Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/v3/process_ratelimit.proto`\\n- Purpose: Rate-limits access log emission using global token buckets\\n\\n### Core/Common Infrastructure\\n\\n#### Access Log Framework (Core)\\n- `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.cc/h`: Core access log filter implementation and factory\\n- `source/common/access_log/access_log_manager_impl.cc/h`: Manages access log instances\\n- Provides: FilterFactory, StatusCodeFilter, DurationFilter, HeaderFilter, ResponseFlagFilter, GrpcStatusFilter, LogTypeFilter, MetadataFilter, and logical operators (AND, OR filters)\\n\\n#### Access Logger Common Base\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/access_log_base.cc/h`: Base class for access logger implementations\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/file_access_log_impl.cc/h`: Core file writing implementation\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger.h`: gRPC logger interface\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger_clients.h`: gRPC client management\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger_utils.cc/h`: gRPC utility functions\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/stream_access_log_common_impl.h`: Base for stream loggers\\n\\n### JSON/Structured Logging Support Summary\\n\\n**Full Structured Logging Support (Recommended):**\\n1. File Logger - Supports plain text, JSON, and typed JSON formats\\n2. Fluentd Logger - JSON with MessagePack serialization for nested objects\\n3. gRPC/ALS Logger - Protobuf-based structured messages\\n4. OpenTelemetry Logger - OTEL protocol with structured attributes and body\\n5. Stream Logger - Can output JSON via SubstitutionFormatString\\n\\n**Implementation-Defined:**\\n- WASM Logger - Format depends on plugin\\n- Dynamic Modules Logger - Format depends on loaded module\\n\\n**Not Applicable:**\\n- Stats Logger - Emits metrics, not logs\\n\\n**Infrastructure/Filtering Only:**\\n- CEL Filter - Controls which requests are logged\\n- Process Rate Limit Filter - Limits log emission rate\\n\\n### Key Observations\\n\\n1. **Modern Format Preference**: Envoy has shifted to `SubstitutionFormatString` (log_format field) as the modern standard for format configuration across File, Stream, and other loggers. This provides unified JSON/text format handling.\\n\\n2. **Structured Data Support**: All primary output loggers (File, Fluentd, gRPC/ALS, OpenTelemetry, Stream) support structured/JSON output. This provides comprehensive observability.\\n\\n3. **Nested Object Support**: Fluentd, gRPC/ALS, and OpenTelemetry support nested JSON objects via command operators like FILTER_STATE and DYNAMIC_METADATA.\\n\\n4. **Protocol-Based vs Text-Based**: gRPC/ALS and OpenTelemetry use binary protocols (gRPC + protobuf or OTLP) for structured data, while File, Fluentd, and Stream can use text-based JSON formats.\\n\\n5. **Extensibility**: WASM and Dynamic Modules provide plugin-based extensibility for custom logging implementations with any format.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

The analysis categorizes each logger by whether it supports structured (JSON) logging or only unstructured text logging.\\n\\n### Access Logger Implementations and JSON/Structured Logging Support\\n\\n#### 1. File Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.file)\\n**Support: YES - Full structured logging support**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/file/config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/file/v3/file.proto`\\n- Supported formats:\\n  - Plain text format (deprecated `format` field)\\n  - JSON format via `json_format` (google.protobuf.Struct, all values as strings)\\n  - Typed JSON format via `typed_json_format` (values as strings, numbers, booleans)\\n  - Modern format via `log_format` (SubstitutionFormatString supporting JSON)\\n- Allows configuration of JSON structures with field substitution using Envoy's command operators\\n\\n#### 2. Fluentd Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.fluentd)\\n**Support: YES - Structured JSON-based logging**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/config.cc`, `fluentd_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/fluentd/v3/fluentd.proto`\\n- Format: Uses JSON formatting (via `createJsonFormatter`) which is then serialized to MessagePack for Fluentd Forward Protocol\\n- Record structure: Defined as `google.protobuf.Struct` with field values derived from access log command operators\\n- Supports nested JSON objects from command operators like FILTER_STATE and DYNAMIC_METADATA\\n\\n#### 3. gRPC Access Log Service (envoy.access_loggers.http_grpc / envoy.access_loggers.tcp_grpc)\\n**Support: YES - Structured protobuf logging**\\n- HTTP Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/http_config.cc`, `http_grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- TCP Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/tcp_config.cc`, `tcp_grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/grpc/v3/als.proto`\\n- Format: Uses StreamAccessLogsMessage protobuf structure containing:\\n  - For HTTP: HTTPRequestProperties, HTTPResponseProperties, and HTTPAccessLogEntry\\n  - For TCP: TCPAccessLogEntry\\n- Inherently structured via protobuf messages (not text-based)\\n- Supports custom tags and filter state object serialization\\n\\n#### 4. OpenTelemetry Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.open_telemetry)\\n**Support: YES - Structured OpenTelemetry protocol logging**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/config.cc`, `access_log_impl.cc`, `http_access_log_impl.cc`, `grpc_access_log_impl.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/open_telemetry/v3/logs_service.proto`\\n- Format: Uses OpenTelemetry Logs Protocol with structured fields:\\n  - `body`: AnyValue field for log message\\n  - `attributes`: KeyValueList for structured key-value pairs\\n  - `resource_attributes`: KeyValueList for resource metadata\\n- Supports both gRPC and HTTP/JSON transports for OTLP export\\n- Values are rendered as strings, numbers, or complex JSON objects via command operators\\n\\n#### 5. Stream Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.stdout / envoy.access_loggers.stderr)\\n**Support: YES - Flexible format support via SubstitutionFormatString**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/stream/config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stream/v3/stream.proto`\\n- Format: Uses `config.core.v3.SubstitutionFormatString` which supports:\\n  - Text format (plain text with substitutions)\\n  - JSON format (via SubstitutionFormatString json_format)\\n- Default format: Envoy's standard text format\\n- Outputs to OS standard output or error streams\\n\\n#### 6. Stats Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.stats)\\n**Support: NO - Not a text or JSON logger**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/stats/config.cc`, `stats.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/stats/v3/stats.proto`\\n- Format: Emits Envoy metrics/counters/histograms, not traditional access logs\\n- Metrics are tagged and values are derived from access log command operators\\n- Not comparable to JSON/structured text logging as it outputs metrics, not logs\\n\\n#### 7. WASM Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.wasm)\\n**Support: Implementation-defined**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/config.cc`, `wasm_access_log_impl.h`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/wasm/v3/wasm.proto`\\n- Format: Determined by the WASM plugin implementation\\n- Envoy passes request/response data and stream info to the WASM VM\\n- The WASM module decides how to format and output logs (could be JSON, text, or other formats)\\n\\n#### 8. Dynamic Modules Access Logger (envoy.access_loggers.dynamic_modules)\\n**Support: Implementation-defined**\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/config.cc`, `access_log.cc`, `access_log_config.cc`\\n- Config Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/dynamic_modules/v3/dynamic_modules.proto`\\n- Format: Determined by the dynamically-loaded module implementation\\n- Envoy loads shared objects (.so files) and passes access log context to the module's implementation\\n- The module can implement any logging format (JSON, text, binary, etc.)\\n- Configuration is passed as google.protobuf.Any and can include format hints (e.g., format: \\\"json\\\")\\n\\n### Access Log Filters (Supporting Infrastructure)\\nThese are filters that determine WHETHER to log, not HOW to format logs:\\n\\n#### 1. CEL Expression Filter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.cel)\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/cel.cc`, `config.cc`\\n- Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/cel/v3/cel.proto`\\n- Purpose: Evaluates CEL expressions to decide if access should be logged\\n\\n#### 2. Process Rate Limit Filter (envoy.access_loggers.extension_filters.process_ratelimit)\\n- Implementation: `source/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/filter.cc`, `config.cc`\\n- Proto: `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/filters/process_ratelimit/v3/process_ratelimit.proto`\\n- Purpose: Rate-limits access log emission using global token buckets\\n\\n### Core/Common Infrastructure\\n\\n#### Access Log Framework (Core)\\n- `source/common/access_log/access_log_impl.cc/h`: Core access log filter implementation and factory\\n- `source/common/access_log/access_log_manager_impl.cc/h`: Manages access log instances\\n- Provides: FilterFactory, StatusCodeFilter, DurationFilter, HeaderFilter, ResponseFlagFilter, GrpcStatusFilter, LogTypeFilter, MetadataFilter, and logical operators (AND, OR filters)\\n\\n#### Access Logger Common Base\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/access_log_base.cc/h`: Base class for access logger implementations\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/file_access_log_impl.cc/h`: Core file writing implementation\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger.h`: gRPC logger interface\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger_clients.h`: gRPC client management\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/grpc_access_logger_utils.cc/h`: gRPC utility functions\\n- `source/extensions/access_loggers/common/stream_access_log_common_impl.h`: Base for stream loggers\\n\\n### JSON/Structured Logging Support Summary\\n\\n**Full Structured Logging Support (Recommended):**\\n1. File Logger - Supports plain text, JSON, and typed JSON formats\\n2. This provides unified JSON/text format handling.\\n\\n2. **Structured Data Support**: All primary output loggers (File, Fluentd, gRPC/ALS, OpenTelemetry, Stream) support structured/JSON output. This provides comprehensive observability.\\n\\n3. **Nested Object Support**: Fluentd, gRPC/ALS, and OpenTelemetry support nested JSON objects via command operators like FILTER_STATE and DYNAMIC_METADATA.\\n\\n4. **Protocol-Based vs Text-Based**: gRPC/ALS and OpenTelemetry use binary protocols (gRPC + protobuf or OTLP) for structured data, while File, Fluentd, and Stream can use text-based JSON formats.\\n\\n5. **Extensibility**: WASM and Dynamic Modules provide plugin-based extensibility for custom logging implementations with any
